## Accepted Decisions

- Scope is `apps/admin-panel` only.
- `apps/client-panel` is out of scope for this umbrella.
- Backend/product docs are read-only source material during discovery.
- Existing auth/session/password/TOTP/settings functionality is a baseline to
  preserve and extend, not rewrite.
- Admin Portal remains internal operator-only.
- Frontend remains a thin client over backend-owned identity, readiness,
  permissions, release, policy, usage, metering and billing state.
- No direct DB/vector DB/model provider/internal backend calls are allowed.
- New domain work should live under `apps/admin-panel/src/modules/<Domain>`.
- API clients and DTO mapping belong in module `api/`; scenario hooks belong
  in module `model/`; route pages belong in `pages/`; UI belongs in `ui/`.
- Shared/package extraction is not justified at this stage.
- Route/navigation items should be added only when the target page is useful
  and non-placeholder.
- This scope requires staged decomposition, not one-stage implementation.
- Conformance review findings 2.1 through 2.8 are incorporated in
  `ADMIN_PORTAL_FRONTEND_UMBRELLA_TZ.md` and `FUNCTIONAL_CHECKLIST.md`.
- Portal-safe read models are primary source for portal summary screens.
- Role vocabulary is `platform_admin`, `platform_operator`,
  `platform_viewer`; backend permissions are preferred when present.
- Agent Config editable schema is fixed for frontend stages.
- Knowledge v1 UX is managed source/document registration, indexing and portal
  readiness, not generic file upload.
- Release manual override, `gate_mode` and manual override visibility are in
  frontend scope.
- Generic domain knowledge setup is handled through template-driven source-pack
  and evaluation markers; AML/KYC is only an accepted backend example/fixture,
  not separate frontend product scope.
- Billing export mutations default to `platform_admin` only unless backend
  permissions explicitly allow more.
- Public widget smoke is an Admin Portal controlled helper/evidence flow using
  `/api/v1/widget/*` and never admin cookies as visitor identity.
- Current `AuthProvider` remains on `/api/admin/v1/users/me` because backend
  documents it as the required alias of `/api/admin/v1/auth/me`; new modules
  use `useAuth` instead of calling either current-admin endpoint directly.
- `/users/me` bootstrap is accepted current implementation, not a
  frontend/backend mismatch. Do not switch to `/auth/me` unless a future
  backend contract explicitly deprecates the alias.
- `/security` must be implemented as a real protected page reusing current
  TOTP/session panels, not as redirect to `/settings?tab=security`.
- Stage 05 fulfilled the root-route gate: authenticated `/` now redirects to
  the real working and tested `/dashboard` route.
- Tenant provisioning v1 uses required visible fields `tenant_name` and
  `external_customer_ref`, optional `external_billing_ref`, and model/API-layer
  `provisioning_correlation_id` plus `idempotency_key`.
- Tenants model/API layer should send `provisioning_correlation_id` in the body
  and use it as `X-Request-ID` where the API helper controls headers.
- Widget install snippet v1 is backend-owned or backend-derived display/copy
  guidance from `public_embed_marker`, `widget_key`, allowed origins and
  site/widget/channel-binding read models.
- New modules must follow current `src/modules/<Domain>/{api,model,pages,ui}`
  structure with public exports through `index.ts`; `pages` and `ui` do not
  call `apiClient` directly.
- Prompt 02 selected staged decomposition, not a one-stage implementation.
- Stage count remains 13 because each stage maps to an independently visible
  frontend increment or final evidence gate.
- Sites/Widgets/Releases remain one stage because release evidence depends on
  the widget channel path and is verified as one publishability increment.
- Usage/Metering/Billing remain one stage because all three share the same
  billing-safe read model boundary and frontend must not duplicate billing
  calculations.
- Prompt 03 accepted the stage package after tightening provisioning
  correlation/idempotency, `AgentKnowledgeBinding` ownership and public widget
  smoke transport isolation.
- Stage 01 `/security` route and shell readiness is accepted after prompt 05.
- Stage 01 documentation sync is complete. App docs now record `/security` as
  part of the current route/menu baseline and keep future Admin Portal sections
  out of the implemented docs.
- Stage 02 Admin Users is accepted after prompt 05. `/admins` is a protected
  implemented page for internal admin user inspection and lifecycle actions.
- Stage 02 documentation sync is complete. App docs now record `/admins`,
  `AdminUsers`, and the implemented `Admin Users` navigation item.
- Stage 03 Navigation And Operator Shell Expansion is accepted after prompt 05.
  AppShell now uses implemented-only navigation groups and permission-aware
  Admin Users visibility.
- Stage 03 documentation sync is complete. App docs now record grouped
  navigation, responsive/collapsed shell behavior and the shell navigation
  recipe.
- Stage 04 Tenants implementation is ready for prompt 05 acceptance review.
  `/tenants` and `/tenants/:tenantId` are protected implemented pages backed
  by real OpenAPI-confirmed tenant portal/provisioning/configuration endpoints.
- Stage 04 Tenants was not accepted in prompt 05. A scoped fix-pass is required
  before docs sync because configuration editing/result feedback are incomplete.
- Stage 04 fix-pass is complete and ready for prompt 05 acceptance review. The
  tenant configuration action now has a controlled JSON edit flow and tenant
  mutations show backend result/correlation feedback.
- Stage 04 Tenants is accepted after repeated prompt 05. `/tenants` and
  `/tenants/:tenantId` satisfy tenant list/detail/provisioning/configuration
  acceptance with controlled config editing and backend mutation
  result/correlation feedback.
- Stage 04 documentation sync is complete. App docs now record `/tenants`,
  `/tenants/:tenantId`, `Tenants`, tenant module ownership, tenant operator
  flow rules and the tenant implementation recipe.
- Stage 05 Dashboard And Operations is accepted after prompt 05. `/dashboard`
  and `/operations` are protected implemented pages backed by live
  OpenAPI-confirmed portal dashboard, operations and platform settings read
  models. Authenticated `/` now redirects to `/dashboard`.
- Stage 05 documentation sync is complete. App docs now record `/dashboard`,
  `/operations`, authenticated `/` -> `/dashboard`, `Operations` module
  ownership, Overview navigation and the read-model overview recipe.
- Stage 06 Agent Templates And Agents implementation is ready for prompt 05
  acceptance review. Tenant-scoped `/tenants/:tenantId/agents`,
  `/tenants/:tenantId/agents/new` and `/tenants/:tenantId/agents/:agentId`
  are protected implemented pages backed by live OpenAPI-confirmed agent
  catalog, portal agent read-model, create, metadata, status, lifecycle,
  setup-checklist, foundation-assessment and channel-binding endpoints.
- Stage 06 Agent Templates And Agents is not accepted after prompt 05. A scoped
  fix-pass is required because agent metadata/status/lifecycle controls are not
  gated by backend `supportedMutationActions`, and raw supported action refs can
  expose future-stage setup actions.
- Stage 06 fix-pass is complete and ready for repeated prompt 05 acceptance
  review. Agent metadata, status and lifecycle controls are now gated by the
  backend read model `supportedMutationActions` through a Stage 06-safe action
  whitelist for the live plural refs `agents.update_metadata`,
  `agents.change_status` and `agents.change_lifecycle`; raw backend action refs
  are no longer rendered in the detail UI.
- Stage 06 Agent Templates And Agents is accepted after repeated prompt 05.
  Tenant-scoped agent catalog/list/create/detail/lifecycle flows are protected,
  backend read-model driven and Stage 06-safe; future setup action refs are not
  exposed as UI actions.
- Stage 06 documentation sync is complete. App docs now record tenant-scoped
  agent routes, `AgentTemplates` and `Agents` module ownership, backend-owned
  agent read models/action refs and the tenant-scoped agent flow recipe.
- Stage 07 Agent Config implementation is ready for prompt 05 acceptance
  review. Tenant-scoped `/tenants/:tenantId/agents/:agentId/config` is a
  protected implemented page backed by live OpenAPI-confirmed AgentConfig
  active/list/detail/draft/validate/activate/rollback endpoints. The editable
  form is limited to approved AgentConfig payload groups, validation result is
  backend-owned, activation requires displayed backend validation evidence, and
  rollback requires target version confirmation.
- Stage 07 Agent Config is not accepted after prompt 05. A scoped fix-pass is
  required because the UI/model exposes draft creation but does not expose the
  required create config version flow backed by
  `POST /api/admin/v1/tenants/{tenant_id}/agents/{agent_id}/configs`.
- Stage 07 Agent Config fix-pass is complete and ready for repeated prompt 05
  acceptance review. The UI/model now exposes a confirmed Create version action
  backed by `POST /api/admin/v1/tenants/{tenant_id}/agents/{agent_id}/configs`,
  uses the approved AgentConfig schema, preserves backend
  `supportedMutationActions` gating and shows backend mutation
  result/correlation feedback through the existing result block.
- Stage 07 Agent Config is accepted after repeated prompt 05. Tenant-scoped
  config inspection, draft creation, create-version, backend validation,
  activation and rollback flows are protected, backend-contract driven and
  Stage 07-safe.
- Stage 07 documentation sync is complete. App docs now record tenant-scoped
  Agent Config route, `AgentConfig` module ownership, backend-owned
  config-version/validation/mutation boundaries and the tenant-scoped Agent
  Config flow recipe.
- Stage 08 Knowledge And Binding implementation is ready for prompt 05
  acceptance review. Tenant-scoped
  `/tenants/:tenantId/agents/:agentId/knowledge` is a protected implemented
  route backed by live OpenAPI-confirmed portal knowledge status/source
  catalog/source detail/release-readiness read models and management endpoints
  for source registration, source metadata/disable, document registration,
  document metadata/disable, indexing start/retry and agent knowledge binding.
  Readiness and release impact are displayed from backend read models only;
  no generic upload, direct vector/provider calls or future Policy/Release UI
  was added.
- Stage 08 Knowledge And Binding is accepted after repeated prompt 05. The
  fix-pass moved source/readiness/document/indexing/retrieval support behavior
  into `Knowledge`, kept `AgentKnowledgeBinding` focused on agent binding,
  moved neutral status/info/mutation UI to `shared/ui`, and added
  support-safe chunks/retrieval/support reconstruction drill-downs.
- Stage 08 documentation sync is complete. App docs now record the
  tenant-scoped Knowledge route, `Knowledge` and `AgentKnowledgeBinding` module
  ownership, backend-owned readiness/retrieval/binding boundaries and the
  tenant-scoped Knowledge flow recipe.
- Stage 09 Capabilities And Policy implementation is ready for prompt 05
  acceptance review. Tenant-scoped
  `/tenants/:tenantId/agents/:agentId/capabilities` and
  `/tenants/:tenantId/agents/:agentId/policy` are protected implemented routes
  backed by live OpenAPI-confirmed capability catalog/assignment and policy
  profile/binding/validation endpoints. Mutation controls are gated by backend
  `supportedMutationActions` plus current admin permissions; readiness,
  policy validation and issues are displayed from backend read models only.
- Stage 09 Capabilities And Policy is not accepted after prompt 05. A scoped
  fix-pass is required because `AgentCapabilities` and `AgentPolicy` import the
  `Agents` API through a cross-feature deep import instead of the public
  `Agents` module export.
- Stage 09 Capabilities And Policy fix-pass is complete and ready for repeated
  prompt 05 acceptance review. `AgentCapabilities` and `AgentPolicy` now import
  `agentsApi` and `PortalAgentDetail` from the public `@/modules/Agents`
  module export, preserving the feature module boundary.
- Stage 09 Capabilities And Policy is accepted after repeated prompt 05.
  Tenant-scoped capability assignment and policy binding/validation flows are
  protected, backend-contract driven and Stage 09-safe after the public module
  import fix-pass.
- Stage 09 documentation sync is complete. App docs now record the
  tenant-scoped Capabilities and Policy routes, `AgentCapabilities` and
  `AgentPolicy` module ownership, backend-owned catalog/assignment/binding/
  validation boundaries and the tenant-scoped Capabilities/Policy flow recipe.
- Stage 10 Sites, Widgets And Releases is accepted after repeated prompt 05.
  Tenant-scoped sites/widgets, backend-derived install guidance, public smoke
  evidence and release management flows are protected, backend-contract driven
  and Stage 10-safe after the manual override comment/install guidance
  fix-pass.
- Stage 10 documentation sync is complete. App docs now record tenant-scoped
  Sites & Widgets and Releases routes, `SitesWidgets` and `Releases` module
  ownership, backend-derived install guidance, isolated public smoke transport
  and backend-owned release readiness/evidence/manual override boundaries.
- Stage 11 Conversations And Support is accepted after prompt 05.
  Tenant-scoped conversation runtime summary, chat list/detail, messages,
  message detail, turns, turn detail, current memory, support evidence refs and
  approved close action are protected, support-safe and Stage 11-scoped.
- Stage 11 documentation sync is complete. App docs now record the
  tenant-scoped Conversations route, `Conversations` module ownership,
  support-safe display boundary, read-only-by-default support inspection,
  approved close action and the tenant-scoped conversation support flow recipe.
- Stage 12 Usage, Metering And Billing Export is accepted after prompt 05.
  Tenant-scoped usage/metering and billing export routes are protected,
  backend read-model driven, permission-aware and Stage 12-scoped; no local
  pricing, invoice, payment, tax or revenue-recognition logic was introduced.
- Stage 12 documentation sync is complete. App docs now record the
  tenant-scoped Usage & Metering and Billing Export routes, `UsageBilling`
  module ownership, backend-owned usage/metering/billing export read models,
  permission-aware billing export mutations and the no-local-pricing/invoice/
  payment/tax boundary.
- Stage 13 End-To-End Smoke, Evidence And Docs Sync is accepted after prompt
  05. The final route smoke fixes the shipped route surface, verifies the
  protected tenant -> agent -> config/knowledge/capabilities/policy ->
  sites/widgets -> releases -> conversations -> usage/billing route journey,
  confirms authenticated `/` redirects to `/dashboard`, and preserves the
  Admin Portal thin-client boundaries with no unresolved frontend blockers.
- Stage 13 documentation sync is complete. App docs already reflected the
  accepted final route smoke, evidence search boundaries and final smoke
  recipe; the adapted prompt package README and pipeline state now point to
  umbrella finalization.
- Backend OpenAPI is the source of truth for API paths. Use `/openapi.json`
  primarily; `/api/v1/openapi.json` remains a compatibility alias.
- Live OpenAPI verified on `2026-05-12`: Stage 01 has no dedicated backend
  security endpoint. Frontend `/security` must use existing
  `/api/admin/v1/auth/*` and `/api/admin/v1/users/me` contracts.
- Urgent Agent Config Operator UX stage is accepted as a post-finalization fix,
  not `stage_14`. It may touch AgentConfig, narrow Agent Detail guidance,
  existing tenant/agent mutation evidence surfaces and narrow reusable
  copy/evidence UI only.
- Urgent Agent Config evidence must show safe backend-returned action,
  resource type/id, result/status, config version when applicable,
  correlation/request id and timestamp. Missing evidence gets explicit
  fallback text; frontend must not invent ids or infer backend-owned state from
  missing fields.
- Urgent Release Evidence Requirements UI is a single post-finalization stage,
  not `stage_14`. It may touch only the existing Releases route/module,
  Releases-focused tests, i18n and docs/ledger unless prompt 03 documents a
  narrow justified reuse need.
- Release evidence requirements, smoke-case matrix, manual override rules and
  publish evidence metadata are backend-owned read-model data. Frontend may
  perform pre-submit completeness guards but must not duplicate release gates
  or define a local smoke-case catalog.
- Urgent Release Retrieval Evidence Operator Flow consistency review is
  accepted as a post-finalization urgent stage, not `stage_14`. Implementation
  may touch only the existing Releases route/module, Releases-focused tests,
  i18n and docs/ledger unless a narrow no-regression router test is needed.
- Backend TZ-SVC-10 is the contract source for release retrieval evidence
  candidate endpoints; the general Admin Portal API README remains read-only
  thin-client boundary context.
- Release retrieval evidence candidates are backend-owned. Frontend must not
  invent retrieval/support references, must not make historical failed releases
  publishable through fake refs, and must keep runtime usage candidate flow as
  a separate accepted evidence source.
- Urgent Agent-Scoped Knowledge Source Read Model consistency review is
  accepted as a post-finalization urgent stage, not `stage_14`. Implementation
  may touch only the existing Knowledge route/module, Knowledge-focused tests,
  i18n and docs/ledger unless a narrow no-regression router test is needed.
- Backend TZ-SVC-11 is the contract source for agent-scoped Knowledge source
  list/detail/release-readiness read routes. Existing source/document/indexing
  mutation contracts remain unchanged unless backend explicitly rejects the
  current payload shape.
- Knowledge source visibility, source detail and release readiness are
  backend-owned. Frontend must not keep created sources visible from mutation
  payloads, browser storage or local readiness calculations unless the
  agent-scoped read model returns them.

## Current Baseline To Preserve

- Login, refresh, logout and logout all.
- Current admin bootstrap through `/api/admin/v1/users/me`.
- Protected routes and anonymous redirect to `/login`.
- AppShell, theme, locale and app settings providers.
- Settings page and real Security page.
- Admin Users page with internal admin list, safe detail, invite/create and
  lifecycle actions.
- Tenants page with portal tenant list, provisioning form, detail view,
  provisioning binding, audit summary, configuration readout and confirmed
  backend-supported tenant actions.
- Dashboard and Operations pages with backend portal read-model summaries and
  implemented-route quick links only.
- Authenticated root redirect `/` -> `/dashboard`.
- Tenant-scoped agent templates and agent lifecycle pages:
  `/tenants/:tenantId/agents`, `/tenants/:tenantId/agents/new` and
  `/tenants/:tenantId/agents/:agentId`.
- Tenant-scoped AgentConfig route:
  `/tenants/:tenantId/agents/:agentId/config`.
- Tenant-scoped Knowledge route:
  `/tenants/:tenantId/agents/:agentId/knowledge`.
- Tenant-scoped Capabilities route:
  `/tenants/:tenantId/agents/:agentId/capabilities`.
- Tenant-scoped Policy route:
  `/tenants/:tenantId/agents/:agentId/policy`.
- Tenant-scoped Sites & Widgets route:
  `/tenants/:tenantId/agents/:agentId/sites-widgets`.
- Tenant-scoped Releases route:
  `/tenants/:tenantId/agents/:agentId/releases`.
- Tenant-scoped Conversations route:
  `/tenants/:tenantId/conversations`.
- Active sessions list and own session revoke.
- Password setup/reset flows.
- Backend mail aliases `/admin/password-setup` and `/admin/password-reset`.
- TOTP status, enrollment, confirm and disable.
- CSRF header handling.
- `error_code` plus compatibility `code` backend error parsing.
- No access/refresh token storage in browser storage.

## Recommended Stage List

1. Security/auth polish and shell readiness.
2. Admin Users.
3. Navigation and operator shell expansion.
4. Tenants provisioning, list and detail.
5. Dashboard and Operations.
6. Agent Templates and Agent lifecycle.
7. Agent Config.
8. Knowledge management, domain source packs and agent knowledge binding.
9. Capabilities and Policy binding.
10. Sites, Widgets, controlled smoke and release management.
11. Conversations and support inspection.
12. Usage, Metering and Billing Export.
13. End-to-end frontend smoke, evidence and docs sync.

Post-finalization urgent fix stages:
- Agent Config Operator UX And Evidence Fix:
  `stages/urgent_stage_agent_config_operator_ux_fix.md`.

  boundaries.

## 2026-05-12 Stage Decomposition

Prompt:
- `02_decompose_umbrella_tz_into_stages`.

Gate result:
- passed. `allowed_next_step` was `02_decompose_umbrella_tz_into_stages`,
  status mapped to prompt 01 completion, blocked findings were `none`, and
  target paths matched.

Stage decision:
- staged, 13 files.

Minimality rationale:
- one stage would hide independent verification boundaries across access,
  tenants, dashboard/operations, agent setup, release/public smoke,
  support/runtime and billing/export;
- splitting further would mostly duplicate route/module/API ownership checks
  inside the same visible increment.

Verification model:
- prompt 03 reviews the full stage TZ package before any implementation;
- prompt 04 implements exactly one accepted stage at a time;
- prompt 05 reviews the implemented stage against its stage TZ;
- prompt 06 syncs docs only after stage acceptance;
- prompt 07 finalizes only after every stage passes;
- prompt 08 generated adapted execution prompts 04/05/06/07.

Allowed next step is now:
- `04_stage_implementation`.

Optional next step is now:
- `none`.

## 2026-05-13 Stage 08 Acceptance Review

Prompt:
- `05_stage_acceptance_review`.

Stage:
- `stage_08_knowledge_binding`
- `/Volumes/Work/PC/ai_admin_panel/apps/admin-panel/docs/tz/admin-portal-frontend/stages/stage_08_knowledge_binding.md`

Gate result:
- passed. `allowed_next_step` was `05_stage_acceptance_review`, the selected
  stage was recorded as ready for acceptance review, changed files and
  implementation notes were present, and blocked findings were `none`.

Findings:
- blocking. Knowledge source/readiness ownership drifted out of the accepted
  module split. Stage 08 assigns filters, managed source registration,
  indexing state and source/readiness UI to `src/modules/Knowledge/{model,ui}`,
  while the implementation keeps that orchestration and rendering in
  `src/modules/AgentKnowledgeBinding/model/useAgentKnowledgeBindingManager.ts`
  and `src/modules/AgentKnowledgeBinding/ui/AgentKnowledgeBindingView.tsx`.
  Required fix: move Knowledge-owned source/readiness state and UI into
  `src/modules/Knowledge/model` and `src/modules/Knowledge/ui`, leaving
  `AgentKnowledgeBinding` to own agent binding behavior and composition through
  public module APIs.
- blocking. `AgentKnowledgeBindingView` deep-imports
  `InfoGrid`, `MutationResultBlock` and `StatusBadge` from
  `src/modules/Agents/ui/AgentShared`, but the app development guide forbids
  one module deep-importing another module's internals. Required fix: either
  move these now-reused neutral primitives to an appropriate shared UI owner,
  or expose a deliberate public API without deep imports if the project chooses
  that dependency direction.
- blocking. Support-safe drill-downs are incomplete. `knowledgeApi` maps chunks,
  retrieval runs and support reconstruction, but the UI only displays chunk and
  retrieval counts; it does not expose support-safe chunks, retrieval runs or
  support reconstruction where returned, which is required by the UI/UX spec
  and functional checklist. Required fix: add Stage 08-safe drill-down UI and
  focused tests, without direct DB/vector/provider calls and without exposing
  unsupported internal content.

Scope verdict:
- partially implemented. The protected
  `/tenants/:tenantId/agents/:agentId/knowledge` route exists, the agent detail
  links to it, and future Capabilities/Policy/Sites/Widgets/Releases routes are
  absent;
- managed source, document, indexing and binding actions exist, but Stage 08
  cannot be accepted because Knowledge module ownership and support-safe
  drill-down requirements are not met.

Runtime behavior verdict:
- loading, empty, error, permission-disabled, mutation progress/result and
  confirmation states are present for the implemented flows;
- readiness/release status is displayed from backend read models and no
  frontend-local readiness calculation was found;
- generic file upload and direct DB/vector/provider calls were not found.

Architecture verdict:
- blocked. API mapping lives in module API layers and pages do not call
  `apiClient`, but source/readiness model/UI ownership is in the wrong module
  and `AgentKnowledgeBindingView` deep-imports feature-internal UI from
  `Agents`.

Frontend/backend responsibility verdict:
- partially accepted. Portal knowledge read models are used for summaries,
  backend mutation result/correlation feedback is displayed, and direct
  DB/vector/provider/internal backend calls were not found;
- the stage still lacks the required support-safe chunks/retrieval/support
  reconstruction drill-down over backend-provided read models.

Checks:
- `npm run test:admin` passed: 42 files, 142 tests;
- `npm run lint:admin` passed;
- `npm run build:admin` passed;
- boundary `rg` checks passed for no generic upload, no direct
  DB/vector/provider calls and no future-stage route links, but confirmed the
  architecture/drill-down findings above.

## 2026-05-13 Stage 04 Acceptance Review

Prompt:
- `05_stage_acceptance_review`.

Stage:
- `stage_04_tenants`
- `/Volumes/Work/PC/ai_admin_panel/apps/admin-panel/docs/tz/admin-portal-frontend/stages/stage_04_tenants.md`

Gate result:
- passed. `allowed_next_step` was `05_stage_acceptance_review`, the selected
  stage was recorded as ready for acceptance review, changed files and
  implementation notes were present, and blocked findings were `none`.

Findings:
- blocking. Tenant configuration editing is incomplete. The detail UI displays
  `configuration.payload` as read-only JSON and exposes `Save configuration`,
  while the model sends the unchanged payload to `PUT /configuration`.
  Required fix: add a controlled approved-config edit flow or remove/disable
  the update action until an approved edit surface exists; keep DTO mapping and
  mutation orchestration in `Tenants/api` and `Tenants/model`.
- blocking. Tenant status/config mutation success feedback does not preserve
  backend mutation result/correlation. Required fix: store the mutation result
  returned by the API/model layer and show correlation/result feedback after
  confirmed actions, while keeping the audit summary display backend-owned.

Scope verdict:
- partially accepted. `/tenants` and `/tenants/:tenantId` are implemented,
  protected and backed by real Stage 04 endpoints;
- no future-stage Dashboard, Agent, Knowledge, Capability, Policy, Widget,
  Release, Conversation, Usage, Metering or Billing routes/actions were added;
- configuration edit/action semantics remain incomplete, so the stage is not
  accepted.

Runtime behavior verdict:
- list, provisioning wizard, detail read models, provisioning binding, audit
  summary, configuration readout, confirmations, loading/empty/error/readonly
  states are present;
- config update is half-wired because there is no editable payload/state before
  `Save configuration`;
- mutation success notices do not show the returned correlation/result.

Architecture verdict:
- accepted for boundaries. `apiClient` usage is isolated to `Tenants/api`;
  pages compose model hooks and UI; UI invokes manager callbacks only; routes

## 2026-05-13 Stage 06 Acceptance Review

Prompt:
- `05_stage_acceptance_review`.

Stage:
- `stage_06_agent_templates_agents`
- `/Volumes/Work/PC/ai_admin_panel/apps/admin-panel/docs/tz/admin-portal-frontend/stages/stage_06_agent_templates_agents.md`

Gate result:
- passed. `allowed_next_step` was `05_stage_acceptance_review`, the selected
  stage was recorded as ready for acceptance review, changed files and
  implementation notes were present, and blocked findings were `none`.

Findings:
- blocking. Agent detail mutation controls are not gated by backend
  `supportedMutationActions`. `AgentDetailView` enables Save metadata, status
  and lifecycle buttons whenever local role/permission allows mutation, and
  `useAgentDetailManager` submits those mutations without checking whether the
  loaded agent detail supports `agents.update_metadata`,
  `agents.change_status` or `agents.change_lifecycle`. Required fix: derive
  per-action availability from the portal detail read model in the model layer,
  disable or hide unsupported actions, and add focused tests for supported and
  unsupported mutation refs.
- blocking. Agent detail renders raw `supportedMutationActions` as visible
  "Backend-supported mutation actions". Backend can return future-stage refs
  such as `agent_config.manage`, `knowledge.binding.manage`,
  `capability.assignments.manage` and `policy.binding.manage`; showing them in
  Stage 06 leaks future setup actions before Config/Knowledge/Policy stages are
  implemented. Required fix: remove the raw action-ref list or filter it to
  Stage 06-safe evidence only, without showing future-stage refs.

Scope verdict:
- partially accepted. Tenant-scoped `/tenants/:tenantId/agents`,
  `/tenants/:tenantId/agents/new` and `/tenants/:tenantId/agents/:agentId` are
  implemented as protected internal operator pages;
- template catalog/detail display, agent list/detail, create flow and
  setup/foundation/channel read sections are present;
- future-stage action refs leak through the raw supported-actions section, so
  the stage is not accepted.

Runtime behavior verdict:
- loading, empty, error and refresh states are present for list/catalog/detail
  surfaces;
- status and lifecycle actions use confirmation before submit;
- mutation result/correlation feedback is present after detail mutations;
- action availability is half-wired because backend-supported mutation refs do
  not control the visible/enabled mutation buttons.

Architecture verdict:
- accepted for boundaries. `Agents/api` and `AgentTemplates/api` own endpoint
  calls and DTO mapping; model hooks own orchestration; pages compose
  `AppShell`, model hooks and UI; pages/UI/model do not call `apiClient`;
  module public exports go through `index.ts`; no speculative shared extraction
  was introduced.

Frontend/backend responsibility verdict:
- partially accepted. Agent list/detail and setup/foundation/channel sections
  use backend read models and no local readiness/billing/provider calculation
  was added;
- rejected for mutation responsibility because backend `supportedMutationActions`
  are displayed but not used as the action source of truth.

Checks:
- `npm run test:admin` passed: 34 files, 119 tests;
- `npm run lint:admin` passed;
- `npm run build:admin` passed.

Allowed next step is now:
- `04_stage_implementation_fix_pass` for `stage_06_agent_templates_agents`.

## 2026-05-13 Stage 07 Acceptance Review

Prompt:
- `05_stage_acceptance_review`.

Stage:
- `stage_07_agent_config`
- `/Volumes/Work/PC/ai_admin_panel/apps/admin-panel/docs/tz/admin-portal-frontend/stages/stage_07_agent_config.md`

Gate result:
- passed. `allowed_next_step` was `05_stage_acceptance_review`, the selected
  stage was recorded as ready for acceptance review, changed files and
  implementation notes were present, and blocked findings were `none`.

Findings:
- blocking. The required create config version flow is missing from the
  UI/model layer. `AgentConfig/api` defines `createAndActivateVersion` for
  `POST /api/admin/v1/tenants/{tenant_id}/agents/{agent_id}/configs`, and the
  Stage 07 TZ/API reference require create draft/new version, but
  `useAgentConfigManager` and `AgentConfigView` expose only `Create draft`,
  validate, activate and rollback. Required fix: add a Stage 07-safe create
  version action using the approved AgentConfig payload schema, preserve backend
  mutation result/correlation feedback, and add focused API/model/UI tests for
  the create-version lifecycle.

Scope verdict:
- partially accepted. `/tenants/:tenantId/agents/:agentId/config` is
  implemented as a protected tenant/agent-scoped internal operator page;
- active config, version list/detail, approved-schema draft form, backend
  validation result display, activation and rollback confirmations are present;
- Knowledge, Capabilities, Policy, Sites, Widgets, Releases, Conversations,
  Usage and Billing routes/actions are absent;
- the stage is not accepted because one required AgentConfig lifecycle action
  is missing.

Runtime behavior verdict:
- loading, empty, error, refresh, readonly/permission-disabled, form validation,
  mutation notice and backend mutation result states are present;
- activation requires a displayed backend validation result for the selected
  config;
- rollback confirmation includes the selected target version;
- create-version runtime behavior is absent because the `POST /configs` helper
  is not reachable from the model/UI.

Architecture verdict:
- accepted for boundaries. `AgentConfig/api` owns endpoint calls and DTO
  mapping; `AgentConfig/model` owns orchestration and backend action-ref
  gating; pages compose `AppShell`, model hooks and UI; UI does not call
  `apiClient`; module public exports go through `index.ts`; no speculative
  shared extraction or duplicate source of truth was introduced.

Frontend/backend responsibility verdict:
- accepted except for the missing create-version action. Config validity uses
  backend validation response; mutation availability is gated by backend
  `supportedMutationActions`; no frontend-local readiness/policy/billing
  calculation or direct DB/vector/provider/internal backend call was added.

  `CopyableValue` behavior for resource id, result/status, version,
  correlation/request fallback, clipboard copy, or evidence secret/token/
  provider/internal-prompt exclusion.

## 2026-05-26 Release Runtime Provider Preflight UI Addendum

Scope:
- Small frontend addendum inside the existing Release Evidence Requirements UI
  work, covering the backend-provided
  `runtime_provider_preflight` read model on the existing Releases screen.

Implementation summary:
- Releases API maps `runtime_provider_preflight.ready` and safe requirement
  fields: `provider_id`, `credential_key`, `credential_configured`,
  `secret_resolvable`, `state` and `required_action`.
- Releases UI shows a compact ready state when runtime provider preflight is
  ready.
- Releases UI shows a warning/blocker state when runtime provider preflight is
  not ready, including safe provider id, credential key, state and required
  action.
- Publish/evidence flow now explains that runtime smoke cannot produce usage
  evidence while provider credentials are not ready.
- Publish usage id fields now show a hint that values must come from
  successful runtime usage and must not be arbitrary strings.
- `credential_configuration_failure` is localized to a human-readable runtime
  credential message.

Security and boundary result:
- No API key, secret value, raw provider payload, provider console/debug info
  or credential input UI was added.
- Frontend remains read-only for runtime provider preflight.
- Release readiness/publish validation remains backend-authoritative.
- No system credential, provider/model catalog, DB/provider/vector debug or
  direct provider management UI was added.

## 2026-05-26 Urgent Release Evidence Requirements UI Acceptance Review

Prompt:
- `05_urgent_release_evidence_requirements_ui_acceptance_review_prompt.md`

Gate result:
- passed. The ledger allowed
  `05_urgent_release_evidence_requirements_ui_acceptance_review`, urgent stage
  implementation notes, changed files and commands were recorded, and blocked
  findings were `none`.

Findings:
- P1: initial release history never reaches UI state after `loadReleases`.
  In
  `/Volumes/Work/PC/ai_admin_panel/apps/admin-panel/src/modules/Releases/model/useReleasesManager.ts`,
  `loadReleases` fetches `nextReleases` and uses it to select the first
  release, but does not call `setReleases(nextReleases)`. As a result the
  existing `/tenants/:tenantId/agents/:agentId/releases` route can show the
  selected release detail while the release history panel still renders
  `releases.empty_list` until a later mutation refresh calls `setReleases`.
  This violates the urgent stage requirement that the release screen continue
  displaying release list/detail state and creates a half-wired initial
  runtime view.

Scope fit:

  publish flows are not implementation scope.

Architecture/reuse result:
- `Knowledge/api` owns endpoint calls, DTO mapping and safe defaults.
- `Knowledge/model` owns loading, selection, source creation evidence,
  backend-confirmed source visibility, document/indexing reloads and readiness
  refresh.
- `Knowledge/ui` owns source list/detail, empty/no-selection guidance,
  disabled controls and backend-owned readiness rendering.
- `Knowledge/pages` keeps route composition only.
- No shared UI extraction or cross-module ownership move is required.
- Pages/UI do not call transport directly.

Degradation-safety result:
- Accepted auth/session/security and Stage 08 Knowledge baseline are preserved.
- Accepted urgent Release Evidence Requirements UI and Release Retrieval
  Evidence Operator Flow are no-regression boundaries.
- No stale mutation-payload, browser storage, local readiness, release,
  policy, billing, metering, pricing or model-routing source of truth is
  allowed.
- No direct DB/vector/provider/internal backend calls are allowed.
- Mutation evidence may expose only safe ids/evidence values; raw source text,
  raw chunks, provider payloads, secrets, internal prompts and backend-internal
  debug payloads remain forbidden.

Backend API doc note:
- `/Volumes/Work/AI_Agents/ai_core/docs/api/portals/admin/README.md` did not
  enumerate the new TZ-SVC-11 agent-scoped Knowledge routes in the searched
  passages. The backend TZ-SVC-11 frontend task is the explicit route contract
  for this urgent package; the API README remains read-only boundary context.
